<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпугивать.html>отпу́гивать</a> (21213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отпуга́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otpugátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пу́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ги<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуск</a> (2517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпускать.html>отпуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otpuskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуск</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ótpusk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуска</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>отпуска́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>отпуско́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>leave, vacation, holiday, furlough
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ежегодный.html>ежего́дный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ježegódnyj ótpusk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">annual leave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуске</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>отпуску</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ v ótpuske/v otpusku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be on leave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">idtí v ótpusk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go on leave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуске</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>отпуску</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v ótpuske/v otpusku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on leave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">декре́тный <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dekrétnyj ótpusk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">maternity leave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долгосрочный.html>долгосро́чный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dolgosróčnyj ótpusk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">leave of long duration</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убывать.html>убыва́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ubyvátʹ v ótpusk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go on leave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увольнение.html>увольне́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">uvolʹnénije v ótpusk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">giving a holiday, granting leave of absence</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увольнять.html>увольня́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">uvolʹnjátʹ v ótpusk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give a holiday, to grant leave of absence</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:числиться.html>чи́слиться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуске</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">číslitʹsja v ótpuske</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be on leave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпуск.html>о́тпуск</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уход.html>ухо́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнком</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ótpusk po uxódu za rebenkom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">child rearing leave</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>issue, delivery, distribution</li>
<li><i>metal</i> tempering</li>

***отпускать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпускать.html>отпуска́ть</a> (3571)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпускать.html>отпуска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otpuskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпустить.html>отпусти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let go, to let off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпускать.html>отпуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шаг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>otpuskátʹ</b> ni na šag</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not let stray one step, not let stir a step from one's side</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to release, to set free
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпускать.html>отпуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>во́лю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpuskátʹ</b> na vólju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set at liberty, to liberate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпускать.html>отпуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порука.html>пору́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpuskátʹ</b> na porúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take bail</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dismiss, to give leave</li>
<li>to supply, to serve, to issue, to give out, to sell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпускать.html>отпуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шутка.html>шу́тку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpuskátʹ</b> šútku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to crack a joke</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпускать.html>отпуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:комплимент.html>комплиме́нты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpuskátʹ</b> kompliménty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make compliments, to pay compliments</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to allot, to assign, to allow, to provide</li>
<li>to slacken, to relax, to turn loose, to loosen</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to remit, to forgive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпускать.html>отпуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грех.html>грехи́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpuskátʹ</b> grexí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give absolution</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(hair or beard)</i> to grow, to let grow</li>
<li><i>(metal)</i> to temper, to draw</li>
<li><i>(pain)</i> to lessen, to ease</li></ol>

***отпустить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпустить.html>отпусти́ть</a> (1327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпустить.html>отпусти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otpustítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпускать.html>отпуска́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let go, to let off</li>
<li>to release, to set free
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпустить.html>отпусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>во́лю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpustítʹ</b> na vólju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set at liberty, to liberate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпустить.html>отпусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порука.html>пору́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpustítʹ</b> na porúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take bail</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dismiss, to give leave</li>
<li>to supply, to serve, to issue, to give out, to sell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпустить.html>отпусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шутка.html>шу́тку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpustítʹ</b> šútku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to crack a joke</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпустить.html>отпусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:комплимент.html>комплиме́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpustítʹ</b> komplimént</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a compliment, to pay a compliment</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to allot, to assign, to allow, to provide</li>
<li>to slacken, to relax, to turn loose, to loosen</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to remit, to forgive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отпустить.html>отпусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грех.html>грехи́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpustítʹ</b> grexí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give absolution</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(hair or beard)</i> to grow, to let grow</li>
<li><i>(metal)</i> to temper, to draw</li>
<li><i>(pain)</i> to lessen, to ease</li></ol>

***отпущенный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпущенный.html>отпу́щенный</a> (1327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпущенный.html>отпу́щенный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otpúščennyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрабатывать.html>отраба́тывать</a> (11892)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отработать.html>отрабо́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otrabótatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрабатывать.html>отраба́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otrabátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отработать.html>отрабо́тать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to work off <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">usually a debt</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отрабатывать.html>отраба́тывать</a></b> карми́ческий <a href = vnd.unilang:долг.html>долг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otrabátyvatʹ</b> karmíčeskij dolg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to work off the karmic debt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to work <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for a certain period of time</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to improve, to polish up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">through testing by identifying and eliminating flaws</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to complete, to perfect <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a certain task</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отработать.html>отрабо́танный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otrabótannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> exhaust</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отработать.html>отрабо́тать</a> (6136)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rabótatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отработать.html>отрабо́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otrabótatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрабатывать.html>отраба́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to work off <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">usually a debt</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отработать.html>отрабо́тать</a></b> карми́ческий <a href = vnd.unilang:долг.html>долг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otrabótatʹ</b> karmíčeskij dolg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to work off the karmic debt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to work <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for a certain period of time</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отработать.html>отрабо́тать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дней</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otrabótatʹ</b> pjatʹ dnej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to work for five days</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to improve, to polish up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">through testing by identifying and eliminating flaws</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to complete, to perfect <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a certain task</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***отравить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отравить.html>отрави́ть</a> (5575)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">travítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отравить.html>отрави́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otravítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отравлять.html>отравля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to poison, to envenom</li>
<li>to spoil</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ра<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>ви́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***отравлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отравлять.html>отравля́ть</a> (14468)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отравить.html>отрави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otravítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отравлять.html>отравля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otravljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отравить.html>отрави́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to poison, to envenom</li>
<li>to spoil
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отравлять.html>отравля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удовольствие.html>удово́льствие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otravljátʹ</b> udovólʹstvije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spoil/mar the pleasure</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отравлять.html>отравля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сознание.html>созна́ние</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otravljátʹ</b> soznánije komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to poison smb's mind</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отравлять.html>отравля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:существование.html>существова́ние</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otravljátʹ</b> suščestvovánije komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make smb's life unbearable</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отражать.html>отража́ть</a> (5069)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отразить.html>отрази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otrazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отражать.html>отража́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otražátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отразить.html>отрази́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to repel, to ward off, to refute, to parry</li>
<li>to reflect, to mirror</li></ol>
